Announcements</div>\n<ul><li>(<em>05/30/2013 yu to all</em>) <b>Free eDelivery Service.</b> We are happy to announce our new free eDelivery\nservice. This service is to help applicants deliver application\nmaterials, including the reference letters, to employers who are\nnot currently using our full online services. It saves applicants in\ndossier delivery costs, simplifies the letter management for the reference writers, and it's totally free for both employers and\napplicants. To use this service, an employer just needs to \n<a href=\"https://academicjobsonline.org/ajo/request/4\">sign up</a>. \nOnce we have verified your identity and approved your request, you can receive any application materials\nelectronically by simply directing applicants to https://academicjobsonline.org/ajo/edelivery/your_group_number in your job ads; and you'll get notified for any new deliveries, and download the application packages in one simple step or set it up to let the system download them for you automatically.\n<!--Applicants, please ask your perspective employers to use our service.\nEmployers, let's all work together to make academic job applications\nless costly for the applicants. [ Employers, you can try it out on the demo server by login as ed@b.c.d. Applicants, you can try as a@b.c.d ]--><br>&nbsp;</li>\n<li>(<em>04/29/2010 yu to all</em>) <b>Institutional Memberships.</b> We are happy\nto announce that we are now offering institution/school level memberships, which\nenable a school or university to sign up for a membership for all its\ndepartments (groups) to use. The\ninstitutional membership represents a significant cost saving over the\nmultiple departmental memberships within the same institution; and it\nenables you to have better control over the whole hiring process at the\ninstitution level, to make sure your institutional hiring\nstandards and data collection requirements are met. For example, you can enroll any numbers of\ndepartments without additional cost,  create a school-wide EEO/AA form and\ncollect all the EEO/AA and EEO compliance data in one place, ensure all job ads follow a\nstandard template or approve all job ads before posting, configure additional questions for all applicants or\nall hiring managers, or export all application data in all groups to\nyour own databases or 3rd party systems via XML feeds systematically. <!--To see more detail, please watch this \n<a href=\"http://academicjobsonline.org/help/academicjobs/videos/list_30_schl\" >short demo</a>. \nYou can try out the features by login using one of the following email addresses: \ngs@b.c.d, gs1@b.c.d or gs2@b.c.d on the demo server.--><br>&nbsp;</li>\n</ul>\n</div><p>\n</p><div class=\"help clr\"><a href=\"https://twitter.com/ajobsonline\"><img src=\"/icons/ajotw.png\" alt=\"AJO twitter list\" style=\"float:left;border:1px solid #890202;border-radius:10px;margin:5px 5px;\"></a><span style=\"color:#890202\">Privacy Policy/Legal Statement</span>:\nSecurity and privacy are our top priorities and we are doing our best to comply with relevant data protection regulations, to preserve your privacy and to make sure\nyour data is available only to the intended parties.
